36:["$","p",null,{"children":["Multiple sources may point to the same file through different paths (e.g., via symlink). 38:["$","p",null,{"children":"The deduplication process first computes identities for all files in parallel, then synchronously scans to remove duplicates:"}]
3a:["$","p",null,{"children":["This design chose ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"realpath"}]," over inode comparison because some filesystems (NFS, ExFAT, container virtual FS) report unreliable inode values. 87:["$","h2",null,{"children":"SkillTool Execution Flow"}]
88:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Execution Modes"}]
89:["$","p",null,{"children":"SkillTool is the sole tool interface through which the model invokes Skills. It supports two execution modes:"}]
e7:T46e,sequenceDiagram
    participant M as Model
    participant ST as SkillTool
    participant V as validateInput
    participant P as checkPermissions
    participant C as call()

    M->>ST: { skill: "simplify", args: "" }
    ST->>V: Verify Skill exists
    V-->>ST: result: true

    ST->>P: Permission check
    alt Safe-attribute Skill
        P-->>ST: allow (auto)
    else Has allow rule
        P-->>ST: allow (rule)
    else Needs user confirmation
        P-->>ST: ask
    end

    ST->>C: Execute Skill

    alt context: 'fork'
        C->>C: executeForkedSkill()
        Note over C: Runs in sub-Agent<br/>Independent token budget
        C-->>ST: { status: 'forked', result: "..." }
    else context: 'inline' (default)
        C->>C: processPromptSlashCommand()
        Note over C: Expands prompt into<br/>current conversation context
        C-->>ST: { status: 'inline', newMessages: [...] }
    end

    ST-->>M: ToolResult

bd:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Portable Patterns"}]
be:["$","p",null,{"children":"Claude Code's three-layer extensibility architecture contains several reusable design patterns:"}]
bf:["$","h3",null,{"children":"1. Markdown-as-Config Pattern"}]
c0:["$","p",null,{"children":"Using Markdown files (with YAML frontmatter) as a configuration carrier:"}]
c2:["$","p",null,{"children":"Advantages of this pattern:"}]
c3:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Human-readable"}],": Non-developers can write and maintain Skills"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Version control friendly"}],": Markdown diffs are clear and intuitive"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Self-documenting"}],": Frontmatter is configuration, body is documentation"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"IDE support"}],": Standard Markdown format with rich editor support"]}],"\n"]}]
c4:["$","h3",null,{"children":"2. Multi-Level Directory Merge Pattern"}]
c5:["$","p",null,{"children":"Loading configuration from multiple directory levels, merging with priority-based deduplication:"}]
c7:["$","p",null,{"children":["This pattern is applicable to any system needing \"global defaults + project overrides\" semantics. Deduplication uses ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"realpath"}]," rather than path string comparison, correctly handling symlink scenarios."]}]
c8:["$","h3",null,{"children":"3. Conditional Activation Pattern"}]
c9:["$","p",null,{"children":"Resources (Skills, rules, etc.) aren't loaded immediately but declare activation conditions that only take effect when matched at runtime:"}]
cb:["$","p",null,{"children":"This pattern is particularly valuable in large projects. It compresses the Skill list from O(N) to O(active) level while maintaining the ability for on-demand discovery."}]
cc:["$","h3",null,{"children":"4. Register-Rather-Than-Import Pattern"}]
cd:["$","p",null,{"children":"Both Bundled Skills and MCP Skill Builders use the pattern of \"registering to a global Map during module initialization rather than importing directly\":"}]
cf:["$","p",null,{"children":"Benefits of this pattern:"}]
d0:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Breaks circular dependencies"}],": The registration module only imports types, not implementations"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Supports lazy loading"}],": Feature-gated Skills use ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"require()"}]," for on-demand loading"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Test-friendly"}],": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"clearBundledSkills()"}]," can reset state"]}],"\n"]}]
d1:["$","h3",null,{"children":"5. Secure Write Pattern"}]
d2:["$","p",null,{"children":"Bundled Skill file extraction demonstrates secure writing best practices:"}]
d4:["$","p",null,{"children":"Four layers of defense:"}]
d5:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Random directory names prevent pre-creation attacks"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"O_EXCL"}]," prevents overwriting existing files"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"O_NOFOLLOW"}]," prevents symbolic link attacks"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["Path normalization + ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":".."}]," checking prevents directory traversal"]}],"\n"]}]
d6:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Summary"}]
d7:["$","p",null,{"children":"Claude Code's three-layer extensibility architecture — Skills, Plugins, MCP — may seem complex, but the underlying logic is clear:"}]
d8:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Unified representation"}],": All extensible capabilities ultimately become the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"Command"}]," type"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Unified entry point"}],": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"SkillTool"}]," is the sole interface through which the model invokes Skills"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Unified dispatch"}],": Regardless of source, Skill execution goes through the same validation, permission checking, and inline/fork decisions"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Differentiated security"}],": Different sources have different trust levels (MCP prohibits shell commands, Plugins require permission confirmation, Bundled auto-allow)"]}],"\n"]}]
d9:["$","p",null,{"children":["The design philosophy of this architecture is: ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"let users define new capabilities through Markdown files, let third parties extend the ecosystem through Plugins and MCP, while maintaining clear security boundaries at every layer"}],". File Skill path conditional activation and dynamic discovery ensure performance in large projects, Bundled Skill lazy extraction and secure writing ensure reliability for binary distribution, and the Plugin two-tier architecture (Built-in + Marketplace) balances out-of-the-box experience with extensibility freedom."]}]
